===	display_relationals() :
===	CONTEXT : ite = it; it and ite relationals
	===	(v1 == v2)	=	true
	===	(v1 != v2)	=	false
	===	(v1 <  v2)	=	false
	===	(v1 <= v2)	=	true
	===	(v1 >  v2)	=	false
	===	(v1 >= v2)	=	true

===	display_relationals() :
===	CONTEXT : it--; it and ite relationals
	===	(v1 == v2)	=	false
	===	(v1 != v2)	=	true
	===	(v1 <  v2)	=	true
	===	(v1 <= v2)	=	true
	===	(v1 >  v2)	=	false
	===	(v1 >= v2)	=	false

	===	(v1 >  v2)	=	false
